- `blofin_get_positions` – list open positions (optional `inst_id`).  
- `blofin_get_equity_summary` – account equity, margin, min‑size at 50x.  
- `blofin_get_account_balances` – futures balances.  
- `blofin_get_trade_insights` – historical trade performance.

- `blofin_research_trading_tactics` – internet search for tactics (`query`).  
- `blofin_ensure_position_tpsl` – add default TP/SL to a position (`inst_id`).  
- `blofin_get_pending_tpsl` – list live TP/SL orders (optional `inst_id`).  
- `blofin_rank_opportunities` – rank tradable USDT perps by momentum/volume/journal (`top_n`, `side`).  
- `crypto_news_search` – get news or, if no EXA API key, return funding + 24h price‑sentiment proxy (`inst_id`, optional `query`).  
- `blofin_get_funding_rate` – current funding rate & crowding bias (`inst_id`).  
- `blofin_get_ticker` – latest ticker (`inst_id`).  
- `blofin_get_universe_snapshot` – scan all assets (`compact` optional).

2. **Sentiment:** The price‑sentiment score (0.3) is low, reinforcing the bearish bias.  
3. **Funding Data Gap:** Without a funding‑rate, we cannot assess crowding bias (long vs. short) for a contrarian signal. The lack of data is due to rate‑limiting and missing API credentials.  

**Actionable Recommendations**

- **Proceed with Caution:** Given the strong recent decline and weak sentiment, a short‑bias trade could be justified, but the absence of funding‑rate data means we lack a key contrarian indicator.  
- **Resolve Funding‑Rate Issue:** Obtain a valid Blofin API key and retry the funding‑rate request (or wait for rate‑limit reset) to determine crowding bias before committing to a position.  
- **Monitor for Catalysts:** Look for any news or events that might explain the drop (e.g., project updates, exchange delistings). If no positive catalyst emerges, the bearish trend may continue.
